  615 00000198         ;
  616 00000198         ;;DIVU
  617 00000198         DIVU    PROC             {R2-R14}
  618 00000198         ; Divider
  619 00000198         ;   Pre condition:  R0 contains the denominator,        
                       R1 contains the numerator
  620 00000198         ;   Post condition: R0 contains the result (quotient),  
                       R1 contains the remainder c flag set if attempted divisi
                       on by 0, clear otherwise
  621 00000198         ; uses subtraction loop till no more divisors can be tak
                       en from what was initialy dividend
  622 00000198         ; allows for easy remainder
  623 00000198         ; c flag set or cleared if a/0 or a/b
  624 00000198         ; Answer=>r0, Remainder=>R1
  625 00000198         
  626 00000198 B404            PUSH             {R2}        ; psuh r2
  627 0000019A 2200            MOVS             R2,#0       ; intialize answer 
                                                            reg (quotient)
  628 0000019C 2800            CMP              R0,#0       ; check for zero di
                                                            v
  629 0000019E D010            BEQ              divZero     ; branch to zero di
                                                            v
  630 000001A0         
  631 000001A0         loopdu
  632 000001A0 4281            CMP              R1,R0       ; compare dividend,



ARM Macro Assembler    Page 15 ex11


                                                             divisor
  633 000001A2 D302            BLO              endLoopdu   ; if dividend<Divis
                                                            or go to endloop st
                                                            age
  634 000001A4 1C52            ADDS             R2,R2,#1    ; increment quotien
                                                            bt (answer)
  635 000001A6 1A09            SUBS             R1,R1,R0    ; dividend - diviso
                                                            r
  636 000001A8 E7FA            B                loopdu      ; loop
  637 000001AA         
  638 000001AA         endLoopdu
  639 000001AA 0010            MOVS             R0,R2       ; remainders in r1,
                                                             answer in r2, so m
                                                            ove answer (quotien
                                                            t) to r0
  640 000001AC BC04            POP              {R2}        ; reset r2
  641 000001AE B403            PUSH             {R0,R1}     ; push r0 and r1 to
                                                             stack (about to us
                                                            e to set C flag)
  642 000001B0 F3EF 8000       MRS              R0,APSR     ; move specials to 
                                                            r0 --C Flag
  643 000001B4 2102            MOVS             R1,#0x2     ; make carry mask (
                                                            gonna be inverted t
                                                            hrough BICS)
  644 000001B6 0709            LSLS             R1,R1,#28
  645 000001B8 4388            BICS             R0,R0,R1    ; apply inverted ca
                                                            rry mask to make ne
                                                            w specials val maki
                                                            ng c=0
  646 000001BA F380 8800       MSR              APSR,R0     ; set specials val 
                                                            to what i made in r
                                                            0
  647 000001BE BC03            POP              {R0,R1}     ; put answer and qu
                                                            otient back in r0 a
                                                            nd r1
  648 000001C0         
  649 000001C0 4770    exit    BX               LR          ; returns right aft
                                                            er loop if a/b, els
                                                            e divZero calls if 
                                                            a/0
  650 000001C2         
  651 000001C2         divZero
  652 000001C2 B403            PUSH             {R0,R1}     ; push r0 and r1, g
                                                            onna use for c flag
                                                             set
  653 000001C4 F3EF 8000       MRS              R0,APSR     ; move specials to 
                                                            r0 --C Flag
  654 000001C8 2102            MOVS             R1,#0x2     ; make mask for car
                                                            ry
  655 000001CA 0709            LSLS             R1,#28
  656 000001CC 4308            ORRS             R0,R0,R1    ; use mask to make 
                                                            specials val with C
                                                            =1
  657 000001CE F380 8800       MSR              APSR,R0     ; move val to speci
                                                            als
  658 000001D2 BC07            POP              {R0,R1,R2}  ; put inputs back i
                                                            n r0 and r1, and re
                                                            set r2
  659 000001D4 E7F4            B                exit        ; return



ARM Macro Assembler    Page 16 ex11


  660 000001D6         
  661 000001D6         
  662 000001D6                 ENDP
